Livability ~51% (family, location, condition, outdoor) · Financial / resale ~49% (price vs local €/m², value judgment, energy, running costs, tenure, legal). Tuned for a live-in home for one adult + a 3-yo, sold in 5–10 years. Price vs local €/m², family, location, energy (incl. upgrade-potential bonus), tenure, running costs and outdoor are computed from the data; value (a condition-adjusted judgment), condition and legal are scored by hand.
Conf. = data-verification confidence: how many of 6 key fields (price, area, WOZ, energy label, ground/tenure, beds) are verified against an independent source. ✓N/6, green ≥5 · amber ≥3 · red <3; ⚠ = a source conflict. Hover for which fields are unverified.

-1% ask		 79 3 1963 B Erfpacht (afgekocht tot 21-11-2061) ? €277 13 7
NEW via Funda digest 18-Jul-2026 (id 80893030). VERIFIED via full Huispedia detail page (best-documented listing in this batch): EUR515,000 k.k., 79 m2 wonen (NEN 2580) + 6.5 m2 balkon + 8 m2 external storage, 4 kamers (3 slaapkamers), 1 badkamer, galerijwoning in the Valkhof complex, bouwjaar 1963, energielabel B, onderhoud binnen/buiten 'Goed'. Ground: voortdurend recht van erfpacht AFGEKOCHT tot 21-11-2061 -- bought-off, ~35-year runway, low near-term legal risk. VvE managed by VvE Beheer Amsterdam, described as 'gezond en actief' with an MJOP in place. WOZ EUR518,000 (peildatum 01-01-2025) -- asking is essentially AT WOZ (-0.6%) and meaningfully below Huispedia's own realistic-value range of EUR549,000-638,000 (-e.g. 'laag in de markt gezet' per Huispedia's own read) -- a genuinely good value signal, though worth asking the agent directly why it's priced under the model range. CONFLICT: VvE monthly cost appears as two different figures on the same Huispedia page -- the structured 'Kenmerken' table says EUR277/month (used as the primary figure here), while the free-text listing description says EUR326.07/month -- verify the exact figure via the VvE jaarrekening before an offer. CONFLICT: an earlier general web search (via a different aggregator) had suggested energy label E for this address, but the authoritative Huispedia detail page (sourced from EP-Online-derived data) clearly shows label B in both the summary badge and the structured Energie section -- B was used as the verified value. FLAG: Huispedia's own 'verborgen prijsaanpassingen' (hidden price history) timeline shows this unit first listed 'Te koop EUR515.000' via Muriel Makelaardij on 21-05-2026, and the page states '20 dagen op de markt' -- i.e. roughly two months before it showed up in today's (18-Jul-2026) Funda 'new listings' digest. This strongly suggests a relisted/refreshed advertisement rather than a genuinely brand-new one -- verify current Funda status and ask the agent about listing history/any prior price changes before assuming this is fresh inventory. Excellent public transport: Amsterdam Zuid station 0.83km, metro Amstelveenseweg nearby; Beatrixpark and Amsterdamse Bos both close by.

Methodology (model v5): Weighted score out of 10, tuned for a live-in home for one adult + a 3-yo (shared custody), sold in 5–10 years. Two clusters — livability ~51%: Family fit & space (17%), Location & commute (15%), Condition (13%), Outdoor space (6%); financial / resale ~49%: Price vs local €/m² (9%), Value judgment (10%), Energy label (10%), Running costs (8%), Tenure / erfpacht (7%), Legal / title risk (5%). v4 change: €/m² now outweighs the raw WOZ premium — Price vs local €/m² is the asking-vs-WOZ premium centred on the property's city median, so WOZ serves only as the location/size-aware normaliser, not a stale absolute anchor. Running costs are the full owner monthly = VvE + heating advance + WOZ-driven owner taxes (OZB ≈0.063% Amstelveen / ≈0.058% Amsterdam + eigenwoningforfait 0.35% × ~37% box-1), so a higher WOZ raises carrying cost. Price vs €/m², family, location, energy, tenure, running costs and outdoor are computed from the underlying data; value (a condition-adjusted judgment overlay: over-priced-for-condition, bidding-war temper), condition and legal are scored by hand against the rubric. Blank criteria renormalise over the ones that are scored. WOZ values are the official 2025 Kadaster LV-WOZ assessments; OZB/forfait are 2025 rates (tunable) — re-check at offer time. v5 change: veto gates — legal <4, Schiphol LIB zone, price >€550k (budget) or 55+ cap the total at 5.4 (⛔, raw score in tooltip): dealbreakers no longer average away. Running costs add the erfpacht canon; a VvE fee <€100/mo without a verified reserve caps the costs score (underfunded-reserve risk). Location blend Emmakade/Zuidas = 70/30. The relvalue city-median baseline is pinned per quarter. All data as of 2026-07-24.
